# <a name="customize-service-fabric-cluster-settings-and-fabric-upgrade-policy"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5597-103">自訂 Service Fabric 叢集設定和網狀架構升級原則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-103">Customize Service Fabric cluster settings and Fabric Upgrade policy</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a5597-104">本文件將告訴您如何為 Service Fabric 叢集自訂各種網狀架構設定和網狀架構升級原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-104">This document tells you how to customize the various fabric settings and the fabric upgrade policy for your Service Fabric cluster.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-105">您可以在入口網站上或使用 Azure Resource Manager 範本來進行自訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-105">You can customize them on the portal or using an Azure Resource Manager template.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-106">並非所有設定都可以透過入口網站使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-106">Not all settings may be available via the portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-107">若下列設定無法透過入口網站使用，請使用 Azure Resource Manager 範本自訂它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-107">In case a setting listed below is not available via the portal customize it using an Azure Resource Manager template.</span></span>
> 

## <a name="customizing-service-fabric-cluster-settings-using-azure-resource-manager-templates"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5597-108">使用 Azure Resource Manager 範本自訂 Service Fabric 叢集設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-108">Customizing Service Fabric cluster settings using Azure Resource Manager templates</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a5597-109">下列步驟說明如何將新設定 *MaxDiskQuotaInMB* 新增至 *Diagnostics* 區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-109">The steps below illustrate how to add a new setting *MaxDiskQuotaInMB* to the *Diagnostics* section.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a5597-110">移至 https://resources.azure.com</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-110">Go to https://resources.azure.com</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="a5597-111">透過展開 [訂用帳戶] -> [資源群組] -> [Microsoft.ServiceFabric] -> <您的叢集名稱>，來瀏覽至您的訂用帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-111">Navigate to your subscription by expanding subscriptions -> resource groups -> Microsoft.ServiceFabric -> Your Cluster Name</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="a5597-112">選取右上角的 [讀取/寫入]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-112">In the top right corner, select "Read/Write"</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="a5597-113">選取 [編輯] 並更新 `fabricSettings` JSON 元素，然後新增新的元素</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-113">Select Edit and update the `fabricSettings` JSON element and add a new element</span></span>

```
      {
        "name": "Diagnostics",
        "parameters": [
          {
            "name": "MaxDiskQuotaInMB",
            "value": "65536"
          }
        ]
      }
```

## <a name="fabric-settings-that-you-can-customize"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5597-114">您可以自訂的網狀架構設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-114">Fabric settings that you can customize</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a5597-115">以下是您可以自訂的網狀架構設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-115">Here are the Fabric settings that you can customize:</span></span>

### <a name="section-name-transactionalreplicator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5597-203">區段名稱︰TransactionalReplicator</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-203">Section Name: TransactionalReplicator</span></span>
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-204">**參數**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-204">**Parameter**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-205">**允許的值**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-205">**Allowed Values**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-206">**指引或簡短描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-206">**Guidance or short Description**</span></span> |
| --- | --- | --- |

| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-212">BatchAcknowledgementInterval</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-212">BatchAcknowledgementInterval</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-213">時間 (秒)，預設值為 0.015</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-213">Time in seconds, default is 0.015</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-214">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-214">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-215">決定複寫器在收到作業後，要等待多久才回傳通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-215">Determines the amount of time that the replicator waits after receiving an operation before sending back an acknowledgement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-216">在此期間所收到的其他作業會透過同一則訊息回傳其通知，以降低網路流量，但可能也會降低複寫器的輸送量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-216">Other operations received during this time period will have their acknowledgements sent back in a single message-> reducing network traffic but potentially reducing the throughput of the replicator.</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-259">MaxAccumulatedBackupLogSizeInMB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-259">MaxAccumulatedBackupLogSizeInMB</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-260">整數，預設值為 800</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-260">Int, default is 800</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-261">指定備份記錄鏈中備份記錄檔的最大累積大小 (MB)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-261">Max accumulated size (in MB) of backup logs in a given backup log chain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-262">如果增量備份會產生導致累積備份記錄檔的備份記錄檔，增量備份要求將會失敗，因為相關完整備份會大於此大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-262">An incremental backup requests will fail if the incremental backup would generate a backup log that would cause the accumulated backup logs since the relevant full backup to be larger than this size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-263">在這個情況下，使用者需要進行完整備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-263">In such cases, user is required to take a full backup.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-264">MaxWriteQueueDepthInKB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-264">MaxWriteQueueDepthInKB</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-265">整數，預設值為 0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-265">Int, default is 0</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-266">核心記錄器可以針對與此複本相關聯之記錄使用的寫入佇列深度上限，此值為整數值，並且會以 KB 為單位來指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-266">Int for maximum write queue depth that the core logger can use as specified in kilobytes for the log that is associated with this replica.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-267">此值是核心記錄器更新期間可處於待處理狀態的位元組數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-267">This value is the maximum number of bytes that can be outstanding during core logger updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-268">此值可為 0 (讓核心記錄器計算出適當值) 或 4 的倍數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-268">It may be 0 for the core logger to compute an appropriate value or a multiple of 4.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-269">SharedLogId</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-269">SharedLogId</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-270">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-270">String</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-271">共用記錄識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-271">Shared log identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-272">此參數是 GUID，每個共用記錄的這個參數都應該是唯一的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-272">This is a guid and should be unique for each shared log.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-273">SharedLogPath</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-273">SharedLogPath</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-274">string</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-274">String</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-275">共用記錄的路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-275">Path to the shared log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-276">如果此值空白，則會使用預設共用記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-276">If this value is empty then the default shared log is used.</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-280">MinLogSizeInMB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-280">MinLogSizeInMB</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-281">整數，預設值為 0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-281">Int, default is 0</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-282">交易記錄檔大小下限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-282">Minimum size of the transactional log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-283">系統將不會允許把記錄檔截斷為低於此設定的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-283">The log will not be allowed to truncate to a size below this setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-284">0 表示複寫器將會根據其他設定決定記錄大小下限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-284">0 indicates that the replicator will determine the minimum log size according to other settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-285">提高這個值會提高執行部分複本和增量備份的可能性，因為這會降低將相關記錄檔記錄截斷的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-285">Increasing this value increases the possibility of doing partial copies and incremental backups since chances of relevant log records being truncated is lowered.</span></span> |

| --- | --- | --- |
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-290">NodeAddresses</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-290">NodeAddresses</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-291">字串，預設值為 ""</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-291">string, default is ""</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-292">不同節點上可用於與命名服務通訊的位址 (連接字串) 集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-292">A collection of addresses (connection strings) on different nodes that can be used to communicate with the the Naming Service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-293">一開始用戶端會隨機選取其中一個位址來連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-293">Initially the Client connects selecting one of the addresses randomly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-294">如果提供了多個連接字串，而且因為通訊或逾時錯誤而導致連接失敗，用戶端便會循序改用下一個位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-294">If more than one connection string is supplied and a connection fails because of a communication or timeout error; the Client switches to use the next address sequentially.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-295">如需重試語意的詳細資料，請參閱命名服務位址的重試區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-295">See the Naming Service Address retry section for details on retries semantics.</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-508">TargetReplicaSetSize</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-508">TargetReplicaSetSize</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-509">整數，預設值為 7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-509">Int, default is 7</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-510">命名服務存放區之每個資料分割的複本集數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-510">The number of replica sets for each partition of the Naming Service store.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-511">增加複本集數目可增加命名服務存放區資訊的可靠性層級，減少因為節點失敗所會遺失之資訊的變更，代價為 Windows Fabric 的負載以及對命名資料執行更新所需的時間量會增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-511">Increasing the number of replica sets increases the level of reliability for the information in the Naming Service Store; decreasing the change that the information will be lost as a result of node failures; at a cost of increased load on Windows Fabric and the amount of time it takes to perform updates to the naming data.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-512">MinReplicaSetSize</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-512">MinReplicaSetSize</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-513">整數，預設值為 3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-513">Int, default is 3</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-514">要完成更新所需寫入到之命名服務複本的數目下限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-514">The minimum number of Naming Service replicas required to write into to complete an update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-515">如果系統中的作用中複本少於此數目，可靠性系統便會拒絕更新命名服務存放區，直到複本還原為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-515">If there are fewer replicas than this active in the system the Reliability System denies updates to the Naming Service Store until replicas are restored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-516">此值不應超過 TargetReplicaSetSize。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-516">This value should never be more than the TargetReplicaSetSize.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-517">ReplicaRestartWaitDuration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-517">ReplicaRestartWaitDuration</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-518">時間 (秒)，預設值為 (60.0 * 30)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-518">Time in seconds, default is (60.0 * 30)</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-519">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-519">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-520">當命名服務複本停止運作時，此計時器就會啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-520">When a Naming Service replica goes down; this timer starts.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="a5597-521">當它到期時，FM 就會開始取代停止運作的複本 (還不會將它們視為遺失)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-521">When it expires the FM will begin to replace the replicas which are down (it does not yet consider them lost).</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-522">QuorumLossWaitDuration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-522">QuorumLossWaitDuration</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-523">時間 (秒)，預設值為 MaxValue</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-523">Time in seconds, default is MaxValue</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-524">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-524">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-525">當命名服務進入仲裁遺失狀態時，此計時器就會啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-525">When a Naming Service gets into quorum loss; this timer starts.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="a5597-526">當計時器到期時，FM 會將停止運作的複本視為遺失，並嘗試復原仲裁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-526">When it expires the FM will consider the down replicas as lost; and attempt to recover quorum.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-527">請注意，這可能會導致資料遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-527">Not that this may result in data loss.</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-571">MaxIndexedEmptyPartitions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-571">MaxIndexedEmptyPartitions</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-572">整數，預設值為 1000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-572">Int, default is 1000</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-573">通知快取中會保持已編製索引狀態以便同步處理重新連線用戶端的空白資料分割數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-573">The maximum number of empty partitions that will remain indexed in the notification cache for synchronizing reconnecting clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-574">任何超過此數目的空白資料分割，都將會以遞增查閱版本順序從索引中移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-574">Any empty partitions above this number will be removed from the index in ascending lookup version order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-575">重新連線用戶端仍可同步處理和接收遺失的空白資料分割更新，但同步處理通訊協定會變得更耗費資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-575">Reconnecting clients can still synchronize and receive missed empty partition updates; but the synchronization protocol becomes more expensive.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-576">GatewayServiceDescriptionCacheLimit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-576">GatewayServiceDescriptionCacheLimit</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-577">整數，預設值為 0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-577">Int, default is 0</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-578">命名閘道之 LRU 服務說明快取中保有的項目數上限 (設為 0 表示沒有限制)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-578">The maximum number of entries maintained in the LRU service description cache at the Naming Gateway (set to 0 for no limit).</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-579">PartitionCount</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-579">PartitionCount</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-580">整數，預設值為 3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-580">Int, default is 3</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-581">要建立之命名服務存放區的資料分割數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-581">The number of partitions of the Naming Service store to be created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-582">每個資料分割都擁有一個與其索引對應的資料分割索引鍵，因此存在資料分割索引鍵 [0; PartitionCount)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-582">Each partition owns a single partition key that corresponds to its index; so partition keys [0; PartitionCount) exist.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-583">增加命名服務資料分割數目會增加命名服務可執行的級別，其方法是減少任何備用複本集所保有的平均資料量，代價則是資源的使用率會增加 (因為必須維持 PartitionCount*ReplicaSetSize 個服務複本)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-583">Increasing the number of Naming Service partitions increases the scale that the Naming Service can perform at by decreasing the average amount of data held by any backing replica set; at a cost of increased utilization of resources (since PartitionCount*ReplicaSetSize service replicas must be maintained).</span></span>|

### <a name="section-name-runasfabric"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5597-601">區段名稱︰RunAs_Fabric</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-601">Section Name: RunAs_Fabric</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1462">MovementPerPartitionThrottleThreshold</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1462">MovementPerPartitionThrottleThreshold</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1463">單位，預設值為 50</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1463">Uint, default is 50</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1464">如果資料分割之複本的平衡相關移動數目，已達到或超過 MovementPerPartitionThrottleCountingInterval 所指出之過去間隔中的 MovementPerFailoverUnitThrottleThreshold，該資料分割不會發生任何平衡相關移動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1464">No balancing related movement will occur for a partition if the number of balancing related movements for replicas of that partition has reached or exceeded MovementPerFailoverUnitThrottleThreshold in the past interval indicated by MovementPerPartitionThrottleCountingInterval.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1465">MovementPerPartitionThrottleCountingInterval</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1465">MovementPerPartitionThrottleCountingInterval</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1466">時間 (秒)，預設值為 600</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1466">Time in seconds, default is 600</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1467">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1467">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1468">表示要追蹤每個資料分割之複本移動 (搭配使用 MovementPerPartitionThrottleThreshold) 的過去間隔時間長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1468">Indicate the length of the past interval for which to track replica movements for each partition (used along with MovementPerPartitionThrottleThreshold).</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1469">PlacementSearchTimeout</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1469">PlacementSearchTimeout</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1470">時間 (秒)，預設值為 0.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1470">Time in seconds, default is 0.5</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1471">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1471">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1472">在放置服務時，至少搜尋這麼長的時間再傳回結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1472">When placing services; search for at most this long before returning a result.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1473">UseMoveCostReports</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1473">UseMoveCostReports</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1474">布林值，預設值為 false</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1474">Bool, default is false</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1475">指示 LB 略過評分函式的成本項目，以便有機會產生大量移動來獲得更平衡的放置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1475">Instructs the LB to ignore the cost element of the scoring function; resulting potentially large number of moves for better balanced placement.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1476">PreventTransientOvercommit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1476">PreventTransientOvercommit</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1477">布林值，預設值為 false</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1477">Bool, default is false</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1478">決定 PLB 是否應立即計算所起始之移動將釋放的資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1478">Determines should PLB immediately count on resources that will be freed up by the initiated moves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1479">根據預設，PLB 可以在相同節點上起始移出和移入，以便能建立暫時性的過量使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1479">By default; PLB can initiate move out and move in on the same node which can create transient overcommit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1480">將此參數設為 true 將會避免這類過量使用，且會停用隨選重組 (也稱為 placementWithMove)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1480">Setting this parameter to true will prevent those kind of overcommits and on-demand defrag (aka placementWithMove) will be disabled.</span></span> |

|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1661">MaxOperationTimeout</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1661">MaxOperationTimeout</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1662">時間 (秒)，預設值為 MaxValue</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1662">Time in seconds, default is MaxValue</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1663">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1663">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1664">在 ClusterManager 上內部處理作業的全域逾時上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1664">The maximum global timeout for internally processing operations on ClusterManager.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1665">MaxTimeoutRetryBuffer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1665">MaxTimeoutRetryBuffer</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1666">時間 (秒)，預設值為 600</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1666">Time in seconds, default is 600</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1667">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1667">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1668">由於逾時而在內部重試時的作業逾時上限為 <Original Timeout> + <MaxTimeoutRetryBuffer>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1668">The maximum operation timeout when internally retrying due to timeouts is <Original Timeout> + <MaxTimeoutRetryBuffer>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1669">會以 MinOperationTimeout 增量來加上額外的逾時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1669">Additional timeout is added in increments of MinOperationTimeout.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1670">MaxCommunicationTimeout</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1670">MaxCommunicationTimeout</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1671">時間 (秒)，預設值為 600</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1671">Time in seconds, default is 600</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1672">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1672">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1673">ClusterManager 和其他系統服務 (也就是，命名服務、容錯移轉管理員等) 之間的內部通訊逾時上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1673">The maximum timeout for internal communications between ClusterManager and other system services (i.e.; Naming Service; Failover Manager and etc).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1674">此逾時值應小於全域 MaxOperationTimeout (因為每個用戶端作業的系統元件之間可能會有多個通訊)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1674">This timeout should be smaller than global MaxOperationTimeout (as there might be multiple communications between system components for each client operation).</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1675">MaxDataMigrationTimeout</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1675">MaxDataMigrationTimeout</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1676">時間 (秒)，預設值為 600</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1676">Time in seconds, default is 600</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1677">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1677">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1678">在網狀架構升級之後，資料移轉復原作業的逾時上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1678">The maximum timeout for data migration recovery operations after a Fabric upgrade has taken place.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1679">MaxOperationRetryDelay</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1679">MaxOperationRetryDelay</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1680">時間 (秒)，預設值為 5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1680">Time in seconds, default is 5</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1681">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1681">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1682">發生失敗時的內部重試延遲上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1682">The maximum delay for internal retries when failures are encountered.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1683">ReplicaSetCheckTimeoutRollbackOverride</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1683">ReplicaSetCheckTimeoutRollbackOverride</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1684">時間 (秒)，預設值為 1200</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1684">Time in seconds, default is 1200</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1685">以秒為單位指定時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1685">Specify timespan in seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1686">如果 ReplicaSetCheckTimeout 設為 DWORD 的最大值，則會以此組態的值加以覆寫以便進行復原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1686">If ReplicaSetCheckTimeout is set to the maximum value of DWORD; then it's overridden with the value of this config for the purposes of rollback.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5597-1687">向前復原所使用的值絕不會遭到覆寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1687">The value used for rollforward is never overridden.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1688">ImageBuilderJobQueueThrottle</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1688">ImageBuilderJobQueueThrottle</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1689">整數，預設值為 10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1689">Int, default is 10</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="a5597-1690">Image Builder Proxy 作業佇列對於應用程式要求的執行緒計數節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5597-1690">Thread count throttle for Image Builder proxy job queue on application requests.</span></span> |
